{
  "API endpoint slug": "weather.current_temperature_drops_below"
}

=== ACTION_DEVELOPER_INFO ===
{
  "API endpoint slug": "heatzy.a-set-auto-mode",
  "Filter code method": "Heatzy.aSetAutoMode.skip(string?: reason)",
  "Runtime method": "runAction(\"heatzy.a-set-auto-mode\", {})"
}

=== FILTERCODE ===

  Heatzy.aSetAutoMode.setDevice("Living Room Thermostat");
} else {
  Heatzy.aSetAutoMode.skip("Temperature in Paris is not below 5°C or location is not Paris.");
}

=== INTENT ===
Send a weekly email digest every Friday at 10:00 AM with the title "SpaceX Weekly News" to subscribers, containing a list of New York Times articles published between Monday and Friday of the same week, where the search term is "SpaceX" and the section is "Business" or "Technology", including the article title, author, blurb, and URL, and an optional image URL if available.

=== TRIGGER_DEVELOPER_INFO ===
{
  "API endpoint slug": "nytimes.new_article_matching_search"
}

=== ACTION_DEVELOPER_INFO ===
{
  "API endpoint slug": "email_digest.send_weekly_email",
  "Filter code method": "EmailDigest.sendWeeklyEmail.skip(string?: reason)",
  "Runtime method": "runAction(\"email_digest.send_weekly_email\", {})"
}

=== FILTERCODE ===
var day = Meta.currentUserTime.day();
if (day !== 5) { // 5 represents Friday
  EmailDigest.sendWeeklyEmail.skip("Today is not Friday.");
}

var searchTerm = "SpaceX";
var section = ["Business", "Technology"];
var articles = [];

// Filter articles based on search term and section
if (Nytimes.newArticleMatchingSearch.Term === searchTerm && section.includes(Nytimes.newArticleMatchingSearch.Section)) {
  var article = {
    title: Nytimes.newArticleMatchingSearch.Title,
    author: Nytimes.newArticleMatchingSearch.Author,
    blurb: Nytimes.newArticleMatchingSearch.Blurb,
    url: Nytimes.newArticleMatchingSearch.ArticleUrl,
    imageUrl: Nytimes.newArticleMatchingSearch.ImageUrl
  };
  articles.push(article);
}

// Set email digest details
EmailDigest.sendWeeklyEmail.setDayOfWeek("Friday");
EmailDigest.sendWeeklyEmail.setTimeOfDay("10:00 AM");
EmailDigest.sendWeeklyEmail.setTitle("SpaceX Weekly News");

// Create message content
var message = "<ul>";
articles.forEach(function(article) {
  message += `<li><a href='${article.url}'>${article.title}</a> by ${article.author}<br>${article.blurb}</li>`;
});
message += "</ul>";

// Add optional image URL if available
if (Nytimes.newArticleMatchingSearch.ImageUrl) {
  message += `<img src='${Nytimes.newArticleMatchingSearch.ImageUrl}'/>`;
}

EmailDigest.sendWeeklyEmail.setMessage(message);

    && Evernote.newNoteInNotebook.Tags.includes("blog")

  "API endpoint slug": "smartthings_v2.switched_on_smartthings"
}

=== ACTION_DEVELOPER_INFO ===
{
  "API endpoint slug": "ewelink.light_switch_action",
  "Filter code method": "Ewelink.lightSwitchAction.skip(string?: reason)",
  "Runtime method": "runAction(\"ewelink.light_switch_action\", {})"
}

=== FILTERCODE ===

var switchName = SmartthingsV2.switchedOnSmartthings.SwitchName;
if (switchName === "Living Room Lamp" &&
    SmartthingsV2.switchedOnSmartthings.SwitchedOnAt.includes("off") &&
    (hour >= 18 || (hour === 17 && minute >= 60)) &&

  Ewelink.lightSwitchAction.setOnoffActQuery("on");
} else {
  Ewelink.lightSwitchAction.skip("Conditions not met.");

=== INTENT ===
Turn on the "Living Room Lamp" device at 07:00 every day and turn it off at 19:00.

=== TRIGGER_DEVELOPER_INFO ===
{
  "API endpoint slug": "date_and_time.every_day_at"
}

=== ACTION_DEVELOPER_INFO ===
{
  "API endpoint slug": "tantiv4.turn_on_off",
  "Filter code method": "Tantiv4.turnOnOff.skip(string?: reason)",
  "Runtime method": "runAction(\"tantiv4.turn_on_off\", {})"
}

=== FILTERCODE ===
var currentTime = DateAndTime.everyDayAt.CheckTime;
var hour = currentTime.hour();

if (hour === 7) {
  Tantiv4.turnOnOff.setDeviceName("Living Room Lamp");
  Tantiv4.turnOnOff.setTurnOnOff(true);
} else if (hour === 19) {
  Tantiv4.turnOnOff.setDeviceName("Living Room Lamp");
  Tantiv4.turnOnOff.setTurnOnOff(false);
} else {
  Tantiv4.turnOnOff.skip("Not the scheduled time.");
}

}

=== ACTION_DEVELOPER_INFO ===
{

  "Filter code method": "Hue.turnOffAllHue.skip(string?: reason)",
  "Runtime method": "runAction(\"hue.turn_off_all_hue\", {})"
}

=== FILTERCODE ===
var hour = Meta.currentUserTime.hour();

  if (Hue.turnOffAllHue !== undefined) {
    Hue.turnOffAllHue.setLights("living room");

    Hue.turnOffAllHue.skip("Unable to turn off lights: Invalid or missing action method.");

  Hue.turnOffAllHue.skip("Condition not met: Either hood ID is incorrect or outside of time range (06:00-22:00).");

=== INTENT ===
Send me an email with the subject "New Article from TechCrunch" and the body containing the entry title, entry URL, and entry content whenever a new article is published in the TechCrunch RSS feed that mentions "Apple", with the email sent to my inbox between 08:00 and 18:00 every day.

=== TRIGGER_DEVELOPER_INFO ===
{
  "API endpoint slug": "feed.new_feed_item"
}

=== ACTION_DEVELOPER_INFO ===
{
  "API endpoint slug": "email.send_me_email",
  "Filter code method": "Email.sendMeEmail.skip(string?: reason)",
  "Runtime method": "runAction(\"email.send_me_email\", {})"
}

=== FILTERCODE ===
var hour = Meta.currentUserTime.hour();
if (hour >= 8 && hour < 18) {
  var entryContent = Feed.newFeedItem.EntryContent;
  var entryTitle = Feed.newFeedItem.EntryTitle;
  var entryUrl = Feed.newFeedItem.EntryUrl;
  if (entryContent.toLowerCase().includes("apple") || entryTitle.toLowerCase().includes("apple")) {
    Email.sendMeEmail.setSubject("New Article from TechCrunch");
    Email.sendMeEmail.setBody("Entry Title: " + entryTitle + "\nEntry URL: " + entryUrl + "\nEntry Content: " + entryContent);
  } else {
    Email.sendMeEmail.skip("Article does not mention Apple.");
  }
} else {
  Email.sendMeEmail.skip("Outside of active hours (8 AM to 6 PM).");
}

}

=== ACTION_DEVELOPER_INFO ===
{
  "API endpoint slug": "wiz.turn_on",
  "Filter code method": "Wiz.turnOn.skip(string?: reason)",
  "Runtime method": "runAction(\"wiz.turn_on\", {})"
}

=== FILTERCODE ===
var sunsetTime = new Date(Weather.sunSets.SunsetAt);
var fifteenMinutesBeforeSunset = new Date(sunsetTime.getTime() - 15 * 60 * 1000);
var currentTime = new Date();

  Wiz.turnOn.setEntity("living room");
  Wiz.turnOn.setMode("warm white");
  Wiz.turnOn.setDimming("75%");
} else {
  Wiz.turnOn.skip("Conditions not met.");

When a new note is created in the "Personal" notebook on Evernote with the tags "important, todo" and containing the keyword "meeting", create a new card on the Trello board "Work Tasks" in the list "To-Do" at the top position, with the note title as the card title, the note body HTML as the card description, and assign it to members @johnDoe and @janeDoe, applying the labels "Urgent" and "High Priority", and attach the note's public URL as a photo.

=== TRIGGER_DEVELOPER_INFO ===
{
  "API endpoint slug": "evernote.new_note_in_notebook"
}

=== ACTION_DEVELOPER_INFO ===
{
  "API endpoint slug": "trello.create_card",
  "Filter code method": "Trello.createCard.skip(string?: reason)",
  "Runtime method": "runAction(\"trello.create_card\", {})"
}

=== FILTERCODE ===
if (Evernote.newNoteInNotebook.Notebook === "Personal"
    && Evernote.newNoteInNotebook.Tags.includes("important")
    && Evernote.newNoteInNotebook.Tags.includes("todo")
    && (Evernote.newNoteInNotebook.Title.includes("meeting") || Evernote.newNoteInNotebook.BodyHTML.includes("meeting"))) {
  Trello.createCard.setBoard("Work Tasks");
  Trello.createCard.setListName("To-Do");
  Trello.createCard.setPos("top");
  Trello.createCard.setTitle(Evernote.newNoteInNotebook.Title);
  Trello.createCard.setDescription(Evernote.newNoteInNotebook.BodyHTML);
  Trello.createCard.setMembers("@johnDoe, @janeDoe");
  Trello.createCard.setLabels("Urgent, High Priority");
  Trello.createCard.setUrl(Evernote.newNoteInNotebook.PublicUrl);
} else {
  Trello.createCard.skip("Note does not match the specified criteria.");
}

=== INTENT ===
Turn off the living room WiZ lamp 10 minutes before sunrise when the current weather condition is Sunny and the temperature is above 18 degrees Celsius.

=== TRIGGER_DEVELOPER_INFO ===
{
  "API endpoint slug": "weather.sun_rises"
}

=== ACTION_DEVELOPER_INFO ===
{
  "API endpoint slug": "wiz.turn_off",
  "Filter code method": "Wiz.turnOff.skip(string?: reason)",
  "Runtime method": "runAction(\"wiz.turn_off\", {})"
}

=== FILTERCODE ===
var sunriseTime = new Date(Weather.sunRises.SunriseAt);
var tenMinutesBeforeSunrise = new Date(sunriseTime.getTime() - 10 * 60 * 1000);
var currentTime = new Date();
var currentCondition = Weather.sunRises.Condition;
var currentTempCelsius = Weather.sunRises.TempCelsius;

if (currentTime >= tenMinutesBeforeSunrise &&
    currentCondition === "Sunny" &&
    currentTempCelsius > 18) {
  Wiz.turnOff.skip("Turning off the living room WiZ lamp 10 minutes before sunrise.");
}

=== INTENT ===
When Tom's Withings Sleep detects that he gets into bed between 22:00 and 23:59, log the date and time (in ISO8601 format) in a new row of the Google Spreadsheet named "Sleep Tracker", with the formatted row containing the values "Date|||Time|||Device User" where Date is the current date (e.g., 2020-07-08), Time is the current time (e.g., 22:45), and Device User is Tom, in the folder path "Health/Withings Data".

=== TRIGGER_DEVELOPER_INFO ===
{
  "API endpoint slug": "WithingsSleep.bedin"
}

=== ACTION_DEVELOPER_INFO ===
{
  "API endpoint slug": "google_sheets.append_to_google_spreadsheet",
  "Filter code method": "GoogleSheets.appendToGoogleSpreadsheet.skip(string?: reason)",
  "Runtime method": "runAction(\"google_sheets.append_to_google_spreadsheet\", {})"
}

=== FILTERCODE ===
var hour = WithingsSleep.bedin.DateandTime.hour();
var minute = WithingsSleep.bedin.DateandTime.minute();
if (hour === 22 || (hour === 23 && minute <= 59)) {
  if (WithingsSleep.bedin.DeviceUser === "Tom") {
    var date = WithingsSleep.bedin.DateandTime.date();
    var time = WithingsSleep.bedin.DateandTime.time();
    GoogleSheets.appendToGoogleSpreadsheet.setFilename("Sleep Tracker");
    GoogleSheets.appendToGoogleSpreadsheet.setPath("Health/Withings Data");
    GoogleSheets.appendToGoogleSpreadsheet.setFormattedRow(date + "|||" + time + "|||Tom");
  } else {
    GoogleSheets.appendToGoogleSpreadsheet.skip("Device user is not Tom.");
  }
} else {
  GoogleSheets.appendToGoogleSpreadsheet.skip("Not between 22:00 and 23:59.");
}

=== INTENT ===
Every time Tom's Nokia Sleep detects you get out of bed between 07:00 and 22:00, the date and time will be logged in a row of a Google Spreadsheet named "Sleep Patterns" with a formatted row containing the date, time, and device user, and saved in the "Health Tracking" folder.

=== TRIGGER_DEVELOPER_INFO ===
{
  "API endpoint slug": "WithingsSleep.bedout"
}

=== ACTION_DEVELOPER_INFO ===
{
  "API endpoint slug": "google_sheets.append_to_google_spreadsheet",
  "Filter code method": "GoogleSheets.appendToGoogleSpreadsheet.skip(string?: reason)",
  "Runtime method": "runAction(\"google_sheets.append_to_google_spreadsheet\", {})"
}

=== FILTERCODE ===
var hour = WithingsSleep.bedout.DateandTime.hour();
if (hour >= 7 && hour < 22) {
  var filename = "Sleep Patterns";
  var formattedRow = WithingsSleep.bedout.DateandTime + "|||" + WithingsSleep.bedout.DeviceUser;
  var path = "Health Tracking";
  GoogleSheets.appendToGoogleSpreadsheet.setFilename(filename);
  GoogleSheets.appendToGoogleSpreadsheet.setFormattedRow(formattedRow);
  GoogleSheets.appendToGoogleSpreadsheet.setPath(path);
} else {
  GoogleSheets.appendToGoogleSpreadsheet.skip("Outside of logging hours (7 AM to 10 PM).");
}

=== TRIGGER_DEVELOPER_INFO ===
{
  "API endpoint slug": "smartthings_v2.new_present_smartthings"
}

=== ACTION_DEVELOPER_INFO ===
{
  "API endpoint slug": "irobot.start_robot",
  "Filter code method": "Irobot.startRobot.skip(string?: reason)",
  "Runtime method": "runAction(\"irobot.start_robot\", {})"
}

=== FILTERCODE ===
if (SmartthingsV2.newPresentSmartthings.DeviceName !== "Bedroom sensor") {
  Irobot.startRobot.skip("Not the Bedroom sensor");
} else {
  var arrivedAt = SmartthingsV2.newPresentSmartthings.ArrivedAt;
  // Assuming presence is no longer detected if ArrivedAt is older than a minute
  var currentTime = new Date();
  var arrivalTime = new Date(arrivedAt);
  var timeDiff = (currentTime - arrivalTime) / 1000 / 60; // in minutes

  if (timeDiff > 1) {
    Irobot.startRobot.setRobotName("Roomba");
  } else {
    Irobot.startRobot.skip("Presence still detected");
  }
}

=== INTENT ===
When the hour with the lowest CO2 intensity in electricity production between 07:00 and 19:00 at Herstedøstervej 23 is reached, change the color of all Philips Hue lights in the living room to green (#008000).

=== TRIGGER_DEVELOPER_INFO ===
{
  "API endpoint slug": "watts.lowcarbon"
}

=== ACTION_DEVELOPER_INFO ===
{
  "API endpoint slug": "hue.set_color_all_hue",
  "Filter code method": "Hue.setColorAllHue.skip(string?: reason)",
  "Runtime method": "runAction(\"hue.set_color_all_hue\", {})"
}

=== FILTERCODE ===
if (Watts.lowcarbon.LocationName === "Herstedøstervej 23" &&
    Meta.currentUserTime.hour() >= 7 &&
    Meta.currentUserTime.hour() <= 19) {
  var lowestCo2Hour = null;
  var lowestCo2Level = Infinity;

  for (var hour = 7; hour <= 19; hour++) {
    var co2Level = Watts.lowcarbon.Co2Level; // Assuming this is an array or object with CO2 levels for each hour
    if (co2Level < lowestCo2Level) {
      lowestCo2Hour = hour;
      lowestCo2Level = co2Level;
    }
  }

  if (Meta.currentUserTime.hour() === lowestCo2Hour) {
    Hue.setColorAllHue.setColor("#008000");
  } else {
    Hue.setColorAllHue.skip("Not the hour with the lowest CO2 intensity.");
  }
}

=== INTENT ===

=== TRIGGER_DEVELOPER_INFO ===
{
  "API endpoint slug": "apilio.ifttt_action_reports"
}

=== ACTION_DEVELOPER_INFO ===
{
  "API endpoint slug": "ewelink.light_switch_action",
  "Filter code method": "Ewelink.lightSwitchAction.skip(string?: reason)",
  "Runtime method": "runAction(\"ewelink.light_switch_action\", {})"
}

=== FILTERCODE ===
var hour = Meta.currentUserTime.hour();
var minute = Meta.currentUserTime.minute();
var eventName = Apilio.iftttActionReports.EventName;
var apilioValue1 = Apilio.iftttActionReports.ApilioValue1;

if (eventName === "good_morning" && hour >= 7 && hour < 8) {
  if (apilioValue1 === "Daytime") {
    Ewelink.lightSwitchAction.setOnoffActQuery("on");
    // Automatically turn off after 30 minutes
    var delay = 30 * 60 * 1000; // 30 minutes in milliseconds
    setTimeout(function() {
      Ewelink.lightSwitchAction.setOnoffActQuery("off");
    }, delay);
  } else {
    Ewelink.lightSwitchAction.setOnoffActQuery("on");
  }
} else {
  Ewelink.lightSwitchAction.skip("Event name or time does not match.");
}

{
  "API endpoint slug": "date_and_time.every_weekday_at"
}

=== ACTION_DEVELOPER_INFO ===
{
  "API endpoint slug": "SAUTER_Cozytouch.launch_action_group",
  "Filter code method": "SAUTERCozytouch.launchActionGroup.skip(string?: reason)",
  "Runtime method": "runAction(\"SAUTER_Cozytouch.launch_action_group\", {})"
}

=== FILTERCODE ===
var time = DateAndTime.everyWeekdayAt.CheckTime;
var dayOfWeek = DateAndTime.everyWeekdayAt.DayOfWeek;
var hour = time.hour();

if ((hour === 7 || hour === 19) && (dayOfWeek === "Monday" || dayOfWeek === "Wednesday" || dayOfWeek === "Friday")) {
  if (hour === 7) {
    SAUTERCozytouch.launchActionGroup.set({ action_group: "Good Morning" });
  } else if (hour === 19) {
    SAUTERCozytouch.launchActionGroup.set({ action_group: "Good Evening" });
  }
} else if ((hour === 7 || hour === 19) && (dayOfWeek === "Tuesday" || dayOfWeek === "Thursday")) {
  if (hour === 7) {
    SAUTERCozytouch.launchActionGroup.set({ action_group: "Good Morning" });
  } else if (hour === 19) {
    SAUTERCozytouch.launchActionGroup.set({ action_group: "Good Evening" });
  }
} else {
  SAUTERCozytouch.launchActionGroup.skip("Not the right time or day");
}

  "API endpoint slug": "THERMOR_Cozytouch.launch_action_group",
  "Filter code method": "THERMORCozytouch.launchActionGroup.skip(string?: reason)",
  "Runtime method": "runAction(\"THERMOR_Cozytouch.launch_action_group\", {})"
}

=== FILTERCODE ===
var time = DateAndTime.everyWeekdayAt.CheckTime;
var hour = time.hour();
var dayOfWeek = DateAndTime.everyWeekdayAt.DayOfWeek;

if ((hour === 7 || hour === 19) && ["Monday", "Tuesday", "Wednesday", "Thursday", "Friday"].includes(dayOfWeek)) {
  if (hour === 7) {
    THERMORCozytouch.launchActionGroup.setActionGroup("Morning");
    THERMORCozytouch.launchActionGroup.setTemperature(20);
  } else if (hour === 19) {
    THERMORCozytouch.launchActionGroup.setActionGroup("Evening");
    THERMORCozytouch.launchActionGroup.setTemperature(20);
  }
} else {
  THERMORCozytouch.launchActionGroup.skip("Not the scheduled time or day.");
}

    HoneywellTotalConnectComfort.setsystemtemperature.setTargetTemperature("72");

=== INTENT ===

=== TRIGGER_DEVELOPER_INFO ===
{
  "API endpoint slug": "date_and_time.every_day_at"
}

=== ACTION_DEVELOPER_INFO ===
{
  "API endpoint slug": "yeelight.change_bright",
  "Filter code method": "Yeelight.changeBright.skip(string?: reason)",
  "Runtime method": "runAction(\"yeelight.change_bright\", {})"
}

=== FILTERCODE ===
var currentTime = DateAndTime.everyDayAt.CheckTime;
var targetTime = "7:00 AM";
if (currentTime.substring(0, 5) === targetTime) {
  Yeelight.changeBright.setBright(1);
  // Gradually increase brightness over 15 minutes
  for (var i = 2; i <= 100; i++) {
    setTimeout(function(bright) {
      Yeelight.changeBright.setBright(bright);
    }, (i - 1) * 9000, i); // 9000 ms = 9 seconds, 15 minutes / 100 steps
  }
} else {
  Yeelight.changeBright.skip("Not 7:00 AM");
}

=== INTENT ===
Every day, deposit an amount into my Monzo pot named "Savings" that corresponds to the number of days left in the year plus one, divided by 100, so on January 1st it's £3.65, on January 2nd it's £3.64, and so on until December 31st when it's 1p, using the pot named "Savings" to store these daily savings.

=== TRIGGER_DEVELOPER_INFO ===
{
  "API endpoint slug": "date_and_time.every_day_at"
}

=== ACTION_DEVELOPER_INFO ===
{
  "API endpoint slug": "monzo.pot_deposit",
  "Filter code method": "Monzo.potDeposit.skip(string?: reason)",
  "Runtime method": "runAction(\"monzo.pot_deposit\", {})"
}

=== FILTERCODE ===
const today = Meta.currentUserTime;

// How many days are there this year?
const days_in_year = today.isLeapYear() ? 366 : 365

const day_of_year = today.format('DDD');

// Figure out how many days are left in the year
const days_left_in_the_year = days_in_year-parseInt(day_of_year);

// Move to pot the number of days left in the year + 1 (so that 1st of Jan is £3.65 and 31st December is 1p)
// Divide by 100 for pence
const amount = (days_left_in_the_year+1) / 100;

Monzo.potDeposit.setAmount(amount.toFixed(2));
Monzo.potDeposit.setPot("Savings");

if (dayOfWeek === "Monday") {
  var amount = parseInt(week_of_year);
  Monzo.potDeposit.setAmount(amount.toFixed(2));
  Monzo.potDeposit.setPot("Weekly Savings");
}

{
  "API endpoint slug": "android_phone.receive_a_phone_call"
}

=== ACTION_DEVELOPER_INFO ===
{
  "API endpoint slug": "welltory.send_event",

  "Runtime method": "runAction(\"welltory.send_event\", {})"
}

=== FILTERCODE ===

    && AndroidPhone.receiveAPhoneCall.DeviceName === "Google Pixel 7"
    && new Date(AndroidPhone.receiveAPhoneCall.OccurredAt).getHours() >= 8
    && new Date(AndroidPhone.receiveAPhoneCall.OccurredAt).getHours() < 18

  Welltory.sendEvent.setDatetime(AndroidPhone.receiveAPhoneCall.OccurredAt);

=== ACTION_DEVELOPER_INFO ===
{
  "API endpoint slug": "google_sheets.append_to_google_spreadsheet",

}
